## Argentina (batch-2 rows 514–1543)

**Fact base (sourced):** Argentina **won** the 2022 WC (beat France 3-3, 4-2 pens; Messi MOTM of the final), **qualified** for 2026 (CONMEBOL). Won 2021 Copa (beat Brazil 1-0, Di María) & 2024 Copa (beat Colombia 1-0; group A = Canada/Chile/Peru — beat **Chile** 1-0, did NOT play Brazil). 2014 WC runners-up (lost final to Germany 1-0, Sabella, Maracanã). 2018 R16 exit (Sampaoli). Lost 2015 & 2016 Copa finals to Chile (pens); Messi briefly retired after 2016. Finalissima won June 2022 (before the WC). FIFA #1 in 2023. 2014 ranking 7th; 2018 5th.

- **Row 514** — 2022 qualifiers across **multiple venues**. ✓
- **Row 517/580** — Training base = **AFA complex, Ezeiza**. ✓
- **Row 518** — **Sampaoli** managed the 2018 WC. ✓

- **Row 520** — **Messi** first to score in 4 WCs (2006/2014/2018/2022). ✓
- **Row 522** — Next Copa final loss after 2015 = **2016**. ✓
- **Row 523/526/527/528/530** — Messi's 2016 retirement followed the **2016 Copa final** (v Chile). ✓
